<user_id>109439875507373064531< /user_id><username>Mark Tapia</username><date>1417819795167<//date>< Rating>
3< /Rating>
< text>
PLEASE READ IF LOOKING INTO RENTING FROM "PUBLIC STORAGE"
First and foremost... This facility and it's employees deserve a "5" Star rating (Kathleen is very good at her job).  They're very helpful and have facilitated any and all requests I've ever had and I'm sure they do the same for all their clients.

The primary issue is with the corporate lease agreement from "Public Storage".  We executed our lease in December, 2013 during a period of promotion for "50% off" all units.  Amazing discount especially for the area.  Now the lease is executed with a "set" monthly rent.  The shady business practice of this lease is that clause 2 titled "Term and Rent" states: "THE MONTHLY RENT, AMOUNTS and type of other fees and/or charges, as well as any other term of this lease/rental agreement, MAY BE ADJUSTED BY OWNER (Public Storage) EFFECTIVE THE MONTH FOLLOWING WRITTEN NOTICE BY OWNER TO OCCUPANT SPECIFYING THE ADJUSTMENT, which such notice shall be given not less than thirty (30) days prior to the first day on which the adjustment shall be effective".
-Q. What exactly does this mean?
-A. Owner ("Public Storage") can "adjust" (raise) the monthly rent (regardless of what was agreed upon at the time of lease execution (move-in) effective a minimum of 30 days from time of written notice on the 1st of that month (Notified of increase March 14, rental increase effective May 1).  Written notice is provided on a post card via mail that looks like "junk mail" (really; one could stipulate that particular form of "notice" for a reason...).

In theory, you could sign a lease with an "agreed upon" dollar amount for your unit and the very next day, they could send you a postcard informing you of a "raised-rate" effective the 1st of the month after 30 day minimum-period and they are legally authorized to do that based on the content of the executed lease agreement.

As mentioned before, this location and staff are tremendous and I have nothing but positive things to say about them.  It's unfortunate that at the time of reviewing the lease, it's not always easy to translate the contents until it's too late and realize the reality of what you've already committed to.

With that said... BEWARE your rate can be adjusted at any time and "Pubic Storage" is very sneaky about it.</text>

< text>
The first unit rented at Public Storage in Anaheim (La Palma Ave) was a very good experience as Javier was greatly helpful, informative and took the time to ensure the facility met our needs. However, it was a week later when another large unit was reserved and after 12 hours of packing and moving our very large furniture we arrived at the facility at 6:05 p.m. (5 minutes after the office closed), we discovered that the unit reserved would not accommodate all of our furniture. I noticed someone was in the office and knocked on the door. Javier stopped closing up for the day, opened the door, and listened to my predicament. Because the "System" was already shut down, he could not input the necessary information to switch units to a larger one. Nonetheless, he took it upon himself to find an available (larger) unit for us and assisted us with opening it and changing all the locks. The next day, we completed all the necessary paperwork (which expedited very quickly!).
The price for the storage units are very competitive in the area, however, it's the personal attention to detail, and courtesy shown by Javier that leads me to highly recommending "Public Storage" on La Palma Ave., in Anaheim!!

Javier is the BEST!!!<//text>

< Text>
Note: We had originally been planning a larger wedding prior to COVID. We ended up doing an elopement/zoom wedding at Albertsons Chapel.
Pros:  The location is clean and beautifully decorated. The green hedge walls and hallway of orchids are stunning and come up beautifully even in Zoom/video. The chapel also has a Nest/video camera that gives your guests a different angle. m I heard later that lots of guests would switch between zoom and that camera to get a better view of the dress.
Cons: I think communication prior to the event could have been a bit better so that we could have better prepared - for example we did not know that we could select and entrance and exit song until we were at the location. A brief FAQ or prep document could have eliminated some of the confusion.
All in all this was a beautiful location that had the technology (and marriage licenses) at its disposal so that this did not feel like a fly by night event but rather something beautiful and meaningful.<//Text>

< Name>
Kris D'Amico< /Name>
<Time>1471228311424< /Time>< Review>
My boyfriend and I got engaged in Dec 15.  We searched for a venue that could provide intimate wedding for small group of guests, offer wedding coordinator, photographer, videographer, officiant, hair/make up, flowers, reception and free parking... yes, after all this is LA.
Some for the cons at the other venues were:
dates we desired were unavailable, tacky setting for more cost, or high cost demand and we would have to spend extra money for photographer, videographer, hair/make up  & wedding reception.
After weeks of research, we found Albertson Wedding Chapel.
When I met Daniel for the first time he was very helpful with showing me the chapel and going over our wants for the wedding.
I knew the moment I walked into the chapel that it was the right place for us.  Interior was modern, filled with a lot of natural light and romantic setting.
Orchid decorations are just so beautifully placed.  We could choose custom color lighting depending on our color theme.  Bridal changing room was tastefully done.  Chairs/table decorations were very pretty.  There's also outdoor terrace where guests can mingle before ceremony and during reception. They also take care of marriage license and certificate for the bride & groom.
Patricia, wedding coordinator who's also the photographer was prompt with e-mails & phone calls.  She always greeted me with welcoming smile and accommodated me with all my requests.  Our ceremony photos were beautifully taken.
After our ceremony, Patricia was very prompt in sending us wedding pictures link.  We couldn't be happier with pictures she took. Patricia just knows how to capture the right moments.

For our wedding, Patricia took care of all details.  There were only a few things we had to do on their to do list that Patricia gave us & they all went smoothly.  The package came with catered food from Maggiano's at the Grove & wedding cake from Sweet Lady Jane.  Cake tasting went without any issues.
Their DJ, Richard was another great addition to the whole experience.  He was always prompt with all inquiries I made & met with me total of 2 times in person just to make sure all songs we selected or he recommended were to our liking.  Richard reviewed every component of wedding, from prior to ceremony, during ceremony and reception.  He went over all the ques for my wedding march.He was very attentive to all my questions and wants.
David, the officiant who wed us at our civil ceremony, made sure he was available for our wedding as well which was important to us.  He contacted us a month prior to see how our wedding plans were going.
Michele and her serving staff for the reception were great.  Many of our guests were very pleased with professional and friendly services they received from the staff.  Even with having to customize our table setting to meet our request, they worked very fast and everything turned out nicely.
Patricia made sure that all components to making successful wedding were taken care of.  Wedding pictures she took were gorgeous, they were so many great ones that we had hard time selecting which ones to frame.
Last but not least, Daniel who is also the videographer did an amazing job capturing videos of important moments.
He has great eye for artistry.  He delivered our wedding video on time.  Even after my several requests for tweaking some details on the video, he did without any hesitation.  His wedding video turned out so nice, it seems like a movie trailer that showed just enough portions of entire event.  And for our friends who couldn't attend, video had enough footages that it was like they were almost there.
We had nothing but a wonderful experience with Albertson Wedding Chapel, Daniel and Patricia made us feel very special & their team did a fabulous job carrying out everything. We are so glad they were there to make our wedding a success.< /Review>

< Review>
I met the man of my dreams.  We dated and fell in love.  We decided to get married and started planning a wedding and our future. We picked a date, October 14, 2016 to be exact. Like any new couple we started thinking about buying a house together and all the other things new couples do.  We found the perfect home and even though we were not married yet, we put in an offer and started the paperwork.  I am a veteran, so we were using a VA Loan.  The VA approved our loan and the weekend before we closed escrow they asked why we were not married.  They requested a letter stating details on why they should approve a loan for x amount of money.  I wrote them a 4 page letter, a pretty dang good one at that!  Sure, we were in the clear we started to feel at ease and pack for a trip to Los Angeles we had planned on taking.  Friday at 10 am they called to let us know they had refused the letter and wanted to see a marriage license before we were to close on the following Tuesday.  We were devastated.  I could not stop crying.  Our family was going to be furious, our friends would be disappointed and besides all of that, how was i going to change the date and finish up all the tiny details for our wedding in a mater of hours?!?!  I did not want a courthouse wedding and memories of being married in a cattle call style.  The courthouse told us to check into wedding chapels.  I started to cry even more; to think about getting married in a Vegas style drive through or a cattle call courthouse.  I do not know which was worse.  I found Albertson Wedding Chapel.  After looking at their website, I called just to get info, having no faith is a chapel style wedding but i was desperate.  I spoke to Patricia and cried the whole time I explained my story.  This woman listened quietly and patiently through my sobs as I explained my situation and all my fears.  Patricia not only immediately got down to business, she started moving things around, giving me direction and a path.  She she gave me times, package options, photo options, flower options, , directions, minutes to and from our hotel we were going to be staying at and told me to have myself and my future husband at the chapel at the designated time and she would take care of everything else.  Patricia agreed that no one should EVER have a memory of their wedding day be at a courthouse that is cold and that we have already had enough stress with the planning of the actual wedding and now this added stress.  She had me spend the day getting a manicure and pedicure, massage and other things while she took care of everything else.  We arrived and everything was perfect.  I actually walked down the isle and we had a priest that brought humor into our ceremony and we felt so at ease and welcomed.  Patricia is my fairy godmother.  This company and Patrica were so wonderful that we are planning to have an actual "fake ceremony" with friends and family on our original wedding date in October with Albertson Wedding Chapel.  The treat you like family and make everything not only stress free, but PERFECT!!!< /Review>

< Text>
My daughter and I went to buy propane at 10pm on a cold January night (Our heater requires propane). There was 2 attendants working at that time. My 15 year old daughter went inside to ask to fill or exchange our tank, the man politely confirmed that they have propane available and asked my daughter to wait a minute as he walked outside to the woman that also worked there and happened to be smoking a cigarette about 2 feet away from the door to enter/exit the store. The woman attendant refused us service, her response to her coworker and my daughter was they have propane but it was too late. Neither my daughter or I pleaded with her or mentioned that we needed it for warmth over night, honestly I was shocked at her refusal, I was annoyed at what I saw at the moment as solely something she couldn‚Äôt be bothered to do. Had she said she was on a break I would have understood and waited for her to be on her shift or returned in 15 minutes to get the propane I needed. I saw no reason a polite 15 year old girl should have been refused service, especially for something that is essential to some people for cooking or warmth etc. I have read some reviews that lead me to believe this attendant commonly treats customers in this manner, perhaps she is better suited for a position where she does not interact with customers. I will not be returning to this station, certainly not at night and not if I see the attendant who didn‚Äôt feel like filling a small propane tank.< /Text>

<review>Normally I go to this location and have been for about a year now. I usually receive a fantastic haircut from the same lady every time, sadly I don't remember her name off the top of my head but she is the energetic funny Asian lady with a new hair color every time I go in, and always enjoy going. Thus, I would give this place 5 stars for her service alone. Sadly, I finally had someone different.

I went in today with my girlfriend to get a haircut. Today was pretty busy and being walkins meant we had to wait till someone was available. About an hour goes by and the lady I normally receive my haircut from is still working on someone so I grow impatient and get my hair cut from the first person available, Ruby. She walks me over and I start explaining how I want my hair cut keeping the same style, feathering and layering it and taking off the bulk on top because of my thick hair. She looks at me and says "So basically you want it layered." I should have pointed out that that wasn't all I wanted but all I could say was okay.

Haircut starts off with her taking a water bottle and trying to dampen my hair to cut it. Somehow she didn't hear me say how thick my hair was, so all I could think to myself was how terrible of an idea that was and how it wasn't going to work. She sprays me twice and then asks if i wanted to receive a shampooing before the cut. I chuckle and say yes please. Once we were at the chairs for the shampoo Ruby starts talking with the lady cutting my girlfriends hair. Now, I'm not the kind of person that cares if you talk to me or not while cutting my hair as long as my hair looks good after. So this doesn't bother me. She finishes and walks me over to the chair and me being the forgetful person I am, I tell her that I also would like just half an inch cut off of the length of my hair. This is where I finally realize the mistake I made not waiting for my normal hair lady.

Ruby clarifies the length by showing how much she would cut off and I said that was good. As she's cutting my hair I see shes doing everything pretty fast for how much hair I have. I look over at the mirror and see she isn't layering or doing anything with the top of my head or sides. She is just taking off the half an inch we just established. Either Ruby is super forgetful like myself or she wasn't paying attention to a word I said. She was so focused on a conversation with an employee that she just complete disregarded anything I had said. Along with this, while cutting the length of my hair Ruby was pushing one side of the scissors into the side of my neck. Not hard enough to cut me or leave a mark but enough pressure to be really uncomfortable and make me feel scared I was going to be cut. After maybe five minutes of hardly doing anything she unbuttons the back of the bib thing and then blow drys the back of my head to the point where it was actually starting to burn me. I don't know if she had the high setting on or if she was really close to my neck with the blower but now I knew I was just being rushed. She didn't care about my haircut, didn't care to listen to what I wanted, didn't care about my safety and clearly just wanted me to be done and out of her chair. Ruby is the kind of person that should not be in customer service. If I hadn't combined my girlfriends haircuts and mine together, which were done by two different people, I wouldn't have given her a tip which would be the first time in a very very long time that I wouldn't have tipped someone. By far the worst experience I have had at any place I have gotten my hair cut.< /review>< Pictures>

<Text>I have lived here for 10 years and I do call this place home. Like any large apt. complex there are always issues but I have always been able to get concerns taken care of with the help of the office staff. I have found that if you treat people the way you want to be treated you get better results.
These apts. were  built in the 70s' and the previous owners never did much to maintain or improve them but we have new owners now. To start there are new double pane windows, new central air and new roofing. I'll be the first to admit that at times it has been a pain to work around all the improvements but with the noise reduction ( windows) and the new air units I have seen a drop in my SMUD bill and a reduction of outside noise. from what I understand there are many more improvements to follow. I think they are trying hard to make this a really nice place to live.

As for the cat situation goes, they have been here since I moved in. Recently steps have been taken to trap and neuter the cats to reduce the overpopulation but it is a ongoing process. if you see a cat with the top of its ear tipped that means it's been neutered. if you remove them all then it opens the area to all new unfixed cats thus more kittens and screaming cats in heat. As with anything such as the repairs and improvements it takes time.

We do have security here and I have read that many haven't seen them but I have talked to and received help from them from time to time. They are mostly here in the evenings and overnight hours and there is a number to call if you need personal assistance.

I have also read that some people think the gift cards are why someone may write a good review. A $5.00 gift card is not worth making up a story. I have always been outspoken and say what I feel and if something needs fixed I ask for it in a polite and professional way and it is taken care of in the same manner.

Rent in Sacramento is sky high now but at least Kensington is trying to make this place worth the money. Like I said before...this is home!< /Text><gmapID>0x809adbdddc84e6f3:0x4e3df29aa2a89f32</gmapID><pics>None<//pics><UserId.>101816815182226574320</UserId.>< rate>

Let me first say that my apartment is beautiful, spacious, and the updated versions of all the apartments look great. However, I have had a few bad experiencing with this apartment in the 5 months is have lived here.
I strongly advise that anyone allergic to animals (cats specifically) do NOT move here. They have feral cats that have taken over the complex. If you have a nice car, it will probably be scratched. There is always paw prints on my car, and i have even seen a guy with a convertible have a cat sleeping on his seat in the morning. When it rains, you can smell the cat urine for days.
If you are on a budget this apartment is not the place you want to move. They do not fully cover water or sewer, so it is added to your rent every month. We were suppose to pay $860 and our rent always ranges form $960 to $1000. It seems that every month our rent is higher.
The apartment floors are very creaky. It gets very annoying especially at night.
Despite these minor problems, there is something more important that urged me to write this review. The management is only concerned about nickel and diming all of the tenants. The do not empathize with anyone and their main focus is what they can do to charge a little bit extra. I have experienced this with them often in the last 5 months. It is very frustrating. With that being said, this is a major concern of mine because we are moving out early next month and have an inspection coming up. They provide a list with prices of each thing that needs to be fixed or cleaned before moving out and how much they will charge you if it is not taken care of. I am aware that this is a normal procedure and everyone must undergo inspections while ending a lease, but I have a bad feeling that we will end up getting charged more then we paid for the deposit. We have taken great care of our apartment while living there, but they literally charge for EVERYTHING. And not reasonable prices. Its like they are trying to make a profit off of you at the same time.
With all this being said, I do not recommend this complex. The appearance of the complex and units do not over weigh the bad.</review>
